	PRE
	Instance : ATTACHMENT 	&	Instance /: Attachment 	&	Attachment__commentsValue : STR 	&	Attachment__commentsValue /:ran(Attachment__comments) 	&	Attachment__dateTimeValue : STR 	&	Attachment__dateTimeValue /:ran(Attachment__dateTime) 	&	Attachment__idValue : STR 	&	Attachment__idValue /:ran(Attachment__id) 	&	Attachment__nameValue : STR 	&	Attachment__nameValue /:ran(Attachment__name) 	&	Attachment__typeValue : STR 	&	Attachment__typeValue /:ran(Attachment__type) 	

	THEN 		Attachment := Attachment \/ {Instance}
 || Attachment__comments:= Attachment__comments \/ {(Instance|->Attachment__commentsValue)}
 || Attachment__dateTime:= Attachment__dateTime \/ {(Instance|->Attachment__dateTimeValue)}
 || Attachment__id:= Attachment__id \/ {(Instance|->Attachment__idValue)}
 || Attachment__name:= Attachment__name \/ {(Instance|->Attachment__nameValue)}
 || Attachment__type:= Attachment__type \/ {(Instance|->Attachment__typeValue)}
	END;
